<div id="review_817318692" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/817318692" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/817318692?book_show_action=true">Jan 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer817318692" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5773268792443463505"><b>3.75 ~ 4 Stars </b><br/><br/>This story was definitely well written, had a nice pace and made me want to apply for a passport and take a trip to Spain unfortunately, I didn’t love it. <br/><br/>I felt Mateo's fall for Vera had a lot to do with his want to reclaim his youth and happiness before he was injured and married...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492410144i/22513832.jpg' width='390' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Despite my feelings, their love seemed to be written in the stars, out of this universe, and all that jazz and I do believe the major majority of friends will love it.<br/><br/>Vera Milles is a twenty-three yea</span>
  <span id="freeText5773268792443463505" style="display:none"><b>3.75 ~ 4 Stars </b><br><br>This story was definitely well written, had a nice pace and made me want to apply for a passport and take a trip to Spain unfortunately, I didn’t love it. <br><br>I felt Mateo's fall for Vera had a lot to do with his want to reclaim his youth and happiness before he was injured and married...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492410144i/22513832.jpg" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Despite my feelings, their love seemed to be written in the stars, out of this universe, and all that jazz and I do believe the major majority of friends will love it.<br><br>Vera Milles is a twenty-three year old tatted astronomy college student. She doesn’t speak Spanish, she doesn’t study business but lands a position teaching conversational English to business professional in a resort? (I found this a bit odd but the author confirms that this possible so check it out friends!) She sets off to Spain and not only falls in love with country but also a very married former football star, now restaurant owner, Mateo Casalles.<br><br>Vera and Mateo’s relationship builds slowly with a friendship and chemistry that has an explosive level of angst. Vera attempts to stifle her blooming feelings but the knowledge that Mateo feels the exact same for her amps up the excitement. A reader may want to know if this book has cheating and the answer is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[YES <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Both characters realize that they are unhappy with their lives and that the other adds everything that they were missing.<br><br> <b>
  <i>"What is love? In English.”<br>I raised my brows. “Love, in English, is love…”<br>“What is it in Spanish?<br>I was so enthralled by his hypnotic eyes, I could barely remember. “Amore?”<br>He shook his head ever so slightly. “No. Love in Spanish is you.”</i>
</b><br><br>While falling in love with Mateo, Vera makes several long lasting friendships and is gutted when the program is over and it’s time for her to return home to Canada. Vera’s attempt at doing the right thing isn’t lost on me. I get how the heart wants what the heart wants while her mind wanted to do the right thing. When Vera later agrees to join Mateo in Spain she takes a huge chance. Can their relationship survive meeting his daughter and wife as well as the press? <br> <br>Sadly, I didn’t fall head over heels for Mateo and Vera’s love connection. Vera was a bit young for my taste and although the author tried to drown a reader in her “guilt” over her affair with a married man, the facts were the facts. Some of Mateo’s actions including his handling of his wife was questionable to me. <br><br>I honestly can’t picture these two characters making it for the long haul, sorry. I think the bigger picture from what I got from the story was her realizing that she was worthy of love too and was just as important in the equation as well as never settling when you could have the opportunity for so much more. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Design your own universe, make your own stars,<br>write your own stories and create<br>your own destiny."</i>
</b> <br><br>I <b>NEEDED</b> Mateo’s pov. I think that I would have given me a better insight into his dealings with his wife as well as his feelings and perhaps I would have fallen for this couple. I needed more than "you’re my Estrella". Don’t get me wrong, I liked the “Star" thing that Mateo kept going back to when he spoke with Vera but by the middle of the story, I was on <b>STAR REFERENCE OVERLOAD</b>.<br><br>This could definitely be a case of I suck and the world will love so go forth and get lost in the stars!<br> <br><i>
  <b>*Thanks to Karina Halle for mailing copy of arc in exchange for an honest review*</b>
</i><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5773268792443463505" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_758976394" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/758976394" />
    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/758976394?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=2014-favorite">2014-favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=arc-netgalley-author">arc-netgalley-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer758976394" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12444193909220187836"><b>☆☆ 5 Shining Stars ☆☆</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396884445i/9198322._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='420' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b> “Love is like a thief, it robs you of all thought and logic and all you have left is a heart that you can only pray is strong enough to survive the rest.”</b>
</i><br/><br/>Karina never ceases to amaze me. I absolutely adore everything she writes. <i>Love, in English</i> is a beautifully crafted, character driven story that will always have a special place in my heart. One of the things I appreciate most about Karina’s style is her ability to create such relatable, visceral characters – they are</span>
  <span id="freeText12444193909220187836" style="display:none"><b>☆☆ 5 Shining Stars ☆☆</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396884445i/9198322._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b> “Love is like a thief, it robs you of all thought and logic and all you have left is a heart that you can only pray is strong enough to survive the rest.”</b>
</i><br><br>Karina never ceases to amaze me. I absolutely adore everything she writes. <i>Love, in English</i> is a beautifully crafted, character driven story that will always have a special place in my heart. One of the things I appreciate most about Karina’s style is her ability to create such relatable, visceral characters – they are flawed, they make mistakes but they are endearing and lovable. Yes, the subject matter is a bit taboo, but its life. Good or Bad. Right or Wrong. Everything comes with a price and a consequence. <br><br>What would you be willing to sacrifice for a true, all-consuming love?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396965185i/9211132._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Vera Miles is a 23 year old, Canadian, astrology student. She is adventurous, wild, tattooed and pierced. She doesn't do emotional attachments, and she certainly doesn't fall in love. But, spending a month is the Spanish countryside, helping Spaniards learn conversational English; she finds more than she could have ever imagined - Mateo.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396965185i/9211133._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mateo Casalles is a 38 year old, Spanish, ex soccer player and he is the completely different from anyone she has ever known, or wanted. He is successful, charming, and refined. But, he is also married…<br><br><i>
  <b> I was in love, in lust, in something with him, and all logic, all facts, all reality, none of that seemed to matter, not to my body and not to my heart. </b>
</i><br><br>I am sure some will be wary of the story line, a younger woman and an older married man – but it is remarkably written. I felt Vera’s struggle, the pain, and the love. Desperately trying to do the moral thing, to resist and deny her feelings for Mateo. I never viewed her as a bad person; she was no villain, simply a person in a very complicated situation. And Mateo, he was a man simply moving through the motions; trapped in an unhappy marriage, trying to do the right thing. But meeting Vera opens his eyes, he finds himself completely captivated by her light and he doesn’t want to let her go.<br><br><i>
  <b>”When I know something, I know it. Now, I know what love is. And I love you. And I cannot imagine going back to the life I had before, because that was no life at all. That was just existing. That was just chasing down the next day so I could feel it pass under me.”</b>
</i><b>He placed his large hand over my heart.<i> “You made me stop chasing days. You made me hold on to them.”</i></b> <br><br>This was a beautiful, emotional journey. A slow building, forbidden romance, that is refreshing and unique. It will evoke a range of emotions, I laughed, cried, and swooned. I was angry, hopeful, and scared. I fell in love with these characters and pulled for them till the end. Now that I have finished, I miss them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396968865i/9211789._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="324" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Recommendation: EVERYONE. Read it and try to resist Vera and Mateo – I couldn't. <br><br><i>***Thank you, Karina Halle, for the arc in exchange for an honest review.***</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12444193909220187836" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_755716236" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/755716236" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755716236?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755716236" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17286383327595123626">Karina Halle mentions in her acknowledgements that she worried that her first romance would be a failure, or that it was boring, or that people wouldn't connect with the characters. Well, Karina Halle...<br/><br/><b>
  <i>There's no need to worry. It. Was. Amazing!</i>
</b><br/><br/>In fact, feel free to write some more...A LOT more! Granted not everyone is going to feel the way I do and that's okay.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392707835ra/8598359.gif' width='400' height='070' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>However, there is one huge, glaring, warning beacon going off and if you've read the blurb, you have a good idea but I'm just going</span>
  <span id="freeText17286383327595123626" style="display:none">Karina Halle mentions in her acknowledgements that she worried that her first romance would be a failure, or that it was boring, or that people wouldn't connect with the characters. Well, Karina Halle...<br><br><b>
  <i>There's no need to worry. It. Was. Amazing!</i>
</b><br><br>In fact, feel free to write some more...A LOT more! Granted not everyone is going to feel the way I do and that's okay.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392707835ra/8598359.gif" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However, there is one huge, glaring, warning beacon going off and if you've read the blurb, you have a good idea but I'm just going to come out and tell you. <b>
  <i>Yes, there is cheating.</i>
</b> If this bothers you in any way, don't read the book. I do think that KH handled it very well, maybe too well...poor Vera beat herself up and then some but still, it is there. Now you just have to decide if it's worth it to read this or not.<br><br>Speaking of Vera...she's a college student looking for a little adventure. She goes to Spain to help teach conversational Spanish and that's where she meets Mateo, who she immediately lusts after but she keeps it to herself...or so she thinks.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398399014i/9409890.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I enjoyed Vera and her journey. She's an interesting character but still young and doesn't always make the best decisions but she tries and that's important. She's also very much aware of who she is...and who she isn't. <br><br>Mateo is very yummy. He is who I would consider a "good" Javier (you know who I'm talking about if you've read KH's Artist Trilogy). But...he is not happy, not since he's been put away in nice, little boxes. What's great about him being older is that he knows what he wants and he will fight for it. <br><br>I loved the sexual tension between Vera and Mateo and of course, I loved all the emotional drama too so that was right up my alley. But I was surprised at how much I enjoyed the awkwardness of everyone learning the languages...it was great at providing some comedic relief. (I will never think of being buzzzzed like a bee the same way.) <br><br>When things <i>finally</i> happened, it was pretty steamy although not very graphic. Still I think that I enjoyed the intimacy between Vera and Mateo much more. Reading about them falling in love was so heartwarming. And I just love that he calls her Estrella. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439786278ra/15884539.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were a lot of great characters in the book and I think KH did a great job in bringing them to life. When the class was over and everyone was saying goodbye, I couldn't help but cry! I felt like I was right there with them. <br><br>And then all the emotions that Vera went through when she was back in Canada was torture but what sweet torture! When Vera kept checking her phone for any emails or texts, it was agony! <br><br>I did have one little issue with Mateo and that's when he was at Isabel's car and Vera saw what she saw...ugh! I don't feel like that was explained or handled well enough and to be honest, I'm still really upset about it! <br><br>The ending was fantastic...I loved the parts on the plane! I could've done with more from the Epilogue but I was happy and I really can't complain. It's a wonderful love story and I hope you'll give it a chance. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/655819.gif" width="400" height="020" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ He slowly turned around. “What is love? In English.” <br><br>I raised my brows. “Love, in English, is love?” <br><br>“What is it in Spanish?” <br><br>I was so enthralled by his hypnotic eyes, I could barely remember. “Amore?” <br><br>He shook his head ever so slightly. “No. Love in Spanish is <i>you</i>.”<br><br>♥ “It used to be more of a life. Then the accident happened. And I met Isabel. She took the chaos that was my life and organized it. She trimmed it, separated it. and put it into these tiny boxes, boxes I was too scared to touch. You, <i>you</i>, Vera, you found those boxes and you opened them up. You ripped them apart. You let the chaos loose, filling my life with energy and stars again.”<br><br>♥ “I am saying,” he said carefully, “that this is not the end of the story. Not the way I am writing it.”<br><br>♥ “Love is like a thief, it robs you of all thought and logic, and all you have left is a heart that you can only pray is strong enough to survive the rest.”<br><br>♥ "It meant <i>everything</i> to me."<br><br>♥ “But love makes you an optimist,” she said. “That is what love is. It is hope for the future. Love doesn’t want you to lose faith, to view the world darkly, to have no hope. Love makes you believe in the impossible. That is the meaning of the word.”<br><br>♥ "Always and infinity."<br><br><br><b>*BR w/Melissa!*</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382473058i/5907725.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17286383327595123626" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_898300813" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/898300813" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/898300813?book_show_action=true">Apr 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Lady Vigilante (Feifei) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/10212063-kayla-at-mybookmuse">Kayla at MyBookMuse</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance">oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=third-time-s-the-charm-romance">third-time-s-the-charm-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=alpha-heroes">alpha-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=douchenugget">douchenugget</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer898300813" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5387268555256957705"><b>3.5 STARS!!</b><br/><br/>I think Karina Halle has shown readers what a versatile writer she is – first she dazzles with fast-paced, action-packed stories such as The Artists trilogy and then a suspenseful horror romance like Donners of the Dead and now with her first contemporary romance. I think from the blurb it’s quite obvious that some form of cheating will occur – whether it be physical, emotional, or both and though it’s a touchy subject I wouldn’t be too worried about that part. I think the author addr</span>
  <span id="freeText5387268555256957705" style="display:none"><b>3.5 STARS!!</b><br><br>I think Karina Halle has shown readers what a versatile writer she is – first she dazzles with fast-paced, action-packed stories such as The Artists trilogy and then a suspenseful horror romance like Donners of the Dead and now with her first contemporary romance. I think from the blurb it’s quite obvious that some form of cheating will occur – whether it be physical, emotional, or both and though it’s a touchy subject I wouldn’t be too worried about that part. I think the author addresses infidelity, cheating, and breaking vows in a very tasteful and respectful manner. Nothing about cheating is glorious; even if finding love is a product, there’ll always be a tainted reminder that the new relationship began on a foundation of deceit. Thus, I really admire the author for writing about such a controversial and forbidden topic and as her first contemporary romance too – that took a lot of guts. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398716907i/9454911._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While this book was exceptionally well-written and handled a taboo subject very well (meaning I didn’t want to smash pumpkin all over the MC’s faces), I didn’t love it. I liked it and the writing was amazing as usual, but there are too many factors stacked up against that one great quality. This book was realistic – <i>to a certain extent.</i> What I considered to be as realistic was the temptation, the breaking of vows, and the guilt trip. Sadly, I never once believed in their love. Call me a cynic but I just simply couldn’t see them in a long-term relationship. Albeit the process of what they went through and the degree to which both gave up certain things tugged at my heartstrings, I was never invested nor convinced of their love. I’ve seen this mentioned in a few other reviews and couldn’t agree more - <b>I NEEDED MATEO’S POV.</b> I needed more than Estrella, stars, and other constellations. I’m sorry, but reading this entire story from Vera’s perspective was incredibly draining and I couldn’t connect with Mateo’s character at all. With this book’s highly complex and multi-faceted premise it’s absolutely necessary (at least for me) to include both main character’s POVs in order to get a fuller sense of the story. Like the scene where he and Vera confront his wife? <i>That</i> was one scene I desperately needed his POV because as of now, I’m struggling to accept his actions there. I also don’t believe in insta-love so the speed at which they fell in love and then subtracting Mateo’s POV didn’t give me much to believe in to begin with. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398716907i/9454912._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I definitely enjoyed the second half more than the first half – it’s not that I don’t like details but I was about to suffocate on all the extra descriptions of this and that in the first half and I just want their fricking story already; cut the extra! But that’s just me and so I was pretty bored there. <br><br>I already knew my rating the moment I finished reading; I just didn’t know what to say to back it up. So...3 stars for the rather mediocre reading experience on my part and the extra half star because I liked this more than I disliked it and because Karina Halle worried that her first romance would be a failure. It wasn’t. <br><br><i>A copy of the book was gifted to me by Kathleen Tucker. Thank you!</i> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5387268555256957705" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_880517597" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/880517597" />
    <a title="Ilze" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12206696-ilze"><img alt="Ilze" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1355328800p2/12206696.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/880517597?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ilze" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ilze" href="/user/show/12206696-ilze">Ilze</a>
      </span>

        rated it

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer880517597" class="readable"

Don't do it or own up to it!<a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ She felt ashamed and guilty, but still </span></span>
  <span id="freeText6688864846062517304" style="display:none">I know I am in a minority here, but I just didn't like it.<br><br><b>How I felt about the story and the writing <br> <img     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_880197726" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/880197726" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/880197726?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11757728-geri-reads?shelf=angst-angst-baby">angst-angst-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11757728-geri-reads?shelf=cheating-a-holes">cheating-a-holes</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer880197726" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9860160661272170112">I was expecting this...<br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=35mgpw3' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399312065ra/9533266.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Instead I got this...<br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=wv1ohd' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399314151ra/9533533.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>For a book who wanted to show readers the gray areas of love, this book is pretty much a cliched black and white. I was up for an unconventional heroine who fell in love with a married man. Not an easy subject to write about but if there's anyone who could have pulled this off, it would have been Karina Halle. I know this author can definitely write edgy and raw. <br/><br/>But no dice. Not even close.<br/><br/>For one, I was bored. Just bored. The first 50% was al</span>
  <span id="freeText9860160661272170112" style="display:none">I was expecting this...<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=35mgpw3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399312065ra/9533266.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Instead I got this...<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=wv1ohd" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399314151ra/9533533.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For a book who wanted to show readers the gray areas of love, this book is pretty much a cliched black and white. I was up for an unconventional heroine who fell in love with a married man. Not an easy subject to write about but if there's anyone who could have pulled this off, it would have been Karina Halle. I know this author can definitely write edgy and raw. <br><br>But no dice. Not even close.<br><br>For one, I was bored. Just bored. The first 50% was all about Mateo and Vera taking seistas and talking about the stars. I was bored. The secondary characters were two dimensional and boring. It was established early on that Mateo and Vera wanted to hump each other. This seems to be okay with everybody except for Lauren. Lauren of course is a <s>bitch</s> bicycle, whereas the people who didn't really bat an eye at Vera and Mateo's eye-fucking were good, decent individuals. In fact, these people assured them that it's okay to cheat on Mateo's wife since you can't stop love. *insert roll eyes here*<br><br>I quickly found out that this was going to be a recurring theme throughout the book. And here in lies my problem. It wasn't really the cheating per se that bothered me. It was how the whole thing was set up. I don't know if it was a conscious decision by the author or it was just an unfortunate coincidence. But there were only two types of characters in this book: the ones who are for Mateo and Vera's relationship, regardless of the fact that he's married, were portrayed as good, non-judgmental people. They were Vera's champion and they were cool about Vera and Mateo getting it on because, you know, its twu lurve and it was written in the stars and all that jazz and everything. And then there's the second group. And these are those people who "disapproved" of their relationship or disapproved of Vera composed of her mother, her sister, Lauren and of course, Isabel. They were lumped together into the judgmental bitches category. It was blatantly obvious from then on what the author wanted to me to feel; hate these characters. These characters deserved to be cheated, hated on because they're judgmental bitches. <br><br>Forget the shades of gray, you won't find those here. It's just another overwrought romanticizing of a cheating husband and his younger mistress. <br><br>Mateo is a one-dimensional character. He's portrayed as perfect in every way except that, oppss, he's married. I'm supposed to sympathize with him because he's stuck in a bad marriage with the worst wife possible with his kid being used as a pawn by said wife when he met Vera. But then as the book progressed, I realized that Mateo is just a guy in the throes of a mid-life crisis. Too early for it, being only 38 years old, but his actions were of that same guy. That guy who is trying so hard to recapture his youth. Mateo is that guy. He wanted to feel young again. He wanted his life back pre-wife with all the parties, the wild nights, the beer, no responsibilities, nada. Every time he calls her estrella and talks about building a new universe with her, I wanted to punch him in the nut. <br><br>A little of his POV might have helped. Probably. But it would have been a better read for me if I saw him at least trying to save his marriage or tried to resist Vera. But he didn't. Mateo was a selfish, whiny prick who preyed on the emotions of an insecure young woman. <br><br>The whole angle on the wife doesn't make sense to me and it's what really bothered me the most. Mateo, aside from being a football player, doesn't seem to have any life plans at all. When he was injured, he got lost. His wife was there and basically organized it for me. And she was vilified for it. She seems to be instrumental in pointing him towards being a businessman, investing in his restaurants but his family made her out to be this fame hungry, gold-digging bitch who is far from being the "perfect" wife. It was insinuated that she shouldn't complain at all since she's far from being the perfect wife. Well, duh! To me, it doesn't make sense. The fact that this book had to vilify the wife in order to justify Mateo cheating was just lazy storytelling. It was too drama-llama for me. Even that confrontation scene was ridiculous and trite. I probably would have liked the story better if it was simply because Mateo and Isabel just grew apart and didn't really have passion in their marriage anymore or that Mateo simply found someone better. I mean, yay for them. Instead, it was the wife's fault, y'all! It was predictable and boring. <br><br>Vera, I actually liked at first. But then she fell in love and she became this whiny, insecure, and immature little girl. I don't blame her for falling in love with a married man but the way she handled herself was annoying. Again, I am inundated with the whole cliche of her family being mean to her. Forget the fact that her mother was right in the first place. She shouldn't have left school and go live with a man who, for all intents and purposes, was still married. But since her mom is a bitch, of course it was okay. The kicker was that Vera herself was a product of divorce due to infidelity. But hey, her mom was a bitch who it was totally okay for Vera not to listen to her.<br><br>Can you sense a theme here?<br><br>Her relationship with her mother wasn't really explored. I was hopeful when Vera went back home after her stint in Spain and meeting Mateo. Maybe she will grow up some and get a whole new perspective on life. But again, nope. Instead, all I got was emo Vera. I had to check and blurb again just to be sure I didn't misread her age. She's 23. I was right. But she acted like a sulking 13 year old. My 12 year old niece acts more mature than her. <br><br>Look, I get that there are characters that are purposely created to annoy the crap out of readers but this was just ridiculous. It didn't serve the story well. Frankly, it didn't make Vera and Mateo likable because it was so obvious that it was done to make the their "love" acceptable. It was disingenuous to portray those who disapproved of her and Mateo's relationship as bitches and those who approved as "good people"? Really? I couldn't really accept that even Mateo's family didn't even blink an eye when they found out that he had Vera in his house even before the divorce was final and he was still battling custody for Chloe Ann. And I'm supposed to believe that these people have Chloe Ann's best interest? <br><br>Even Josh, her brother, who I thought was the only sensible person in this whole debacle, disappointed me. That whole justification about divorce was insulting. And Vera, the nit-wit became this pathetic character who bailed after things got too hard. Boohoo! Really pathetic. Where was this free-spirited girl the blurb talked about. She was nowhere to be found.<br><br>But my ire is probably reserve for fucking Claudia. Good God, no wonder Vera is a mess. This woman was an enabler of bad behavior and I'm supposed to like her? It was also telling how the women were portrayed in this book. Generally, those who disapproved of her Vera and Mateo were women. The men were jealous of Mateo because his tattooed mistress while the women looked on with disdain. Now, I don't know why but that really irked me. <br><br>Overall, I found this book just lacking. Lacking in depth, lacking in sensitivity, and lacking in perspective. Mateo's ardent decelerations of love for Vera, his star, and universe had me rolling my eyes too much. Overly romanticizing cheating assholes is not my thing. And Mateo is just that. You may dress him up, pretty him and put beautiful words in his mouth but it doesn't change a thing about him. I'd rather have an honest portrayal of him as a flawed human being who cheated and get his comeuppance first before getting his HEA. But this book portrayed him as anything but. Same with Vera. Her issues were supposed to make me sympathize but it ended up annoying me most of the time. <br><br>To me, this book tried too hard to sell Vera and Mateo's love for each other as acceptable and okay. I generally don't like to be forced into feeling something for certain characters. Not to say that no one can convince me but it has to be an organic thing for me, you know. I wanted to root for them because they deserved it. But it seemed to me like the only way the author knew how to do it was to make some people the villain, which doesn't make sense to me because I thought the whole point of the book is to show that when it comes to matters of the heart, there are no villains. Not Vera or Mateo and certainly not the wife also. I was wrong.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9860160661272170112" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755543577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8381541444872741781"><i>Thank you to the author for providing me a free copy of this book in exchange for an honest review.</i><br/><br/><blockquote>★★★★★ <b>5 STARS</b> ★★★★★</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397794903i/9329292.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Desire. Loss. Hope. Love.</b><br/><br/>Just like our main character ... this book is a <i>brilliant, shining star.</i> It is without doubt Karina Halle’s best work. I am still reeling from the staggering amount of true emotion this book was able to evoke. <br/><br/><b>Tears!</b> I cried, big stupid tears … I yelled … I laughed … I swooned. And I will never think of a siesta the same way again! <br/><br/><i>sigh</i><br/><br/>It was so very <b>perf</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8381541444872741781" style="display:none"><i>Thank you to the author for providing me a free copy of this book in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><blockquote>★★★★★ <b>5 STARS</b> ★★★★★</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397794903i/9329292.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Desire. Loss. Hope. Love.</b><br><br>Just like our main character ... this book is a <i>brilliant, shining star.</i> It is without doubt Karina Halle’s best work. I am still reeling from the staggering amount of true emotion this book was able to evoke. <br><br><b>Tears!</b> I cried, big stupid tears … I yelled … I laughed … I swooned. And I will never think of a siesta the same way again! <br><br><i>sigh</i><br><br>It was so very <b>perfect</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397139589i/9236405._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Vera</b> is a 23 year old student who goes to Spain for the summer to teach english. On her first day in the program she meets 38 year old married businessman, <b>Mateo</b>. <br>From the moment these two meet there is an attraction. What develops between them goes beyond physical … beyond emotional … it is a connection of souls.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397140800i/9236525._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Karina Halle takes what most consider an uncomfortable, even taboo topic and turns it into a <b>beautiful work of art</b>. I never thought I would find myself empathizing with an adulterer ... but ohmygawd! <b>I was routing for them!</b> It takes a lot of talent to change someone's perception on such a heavy issue.<br><br>There is so more to this story than a simple forbidden love. It brings to question the nature of life and happiness. <br><br>What risks are worth taking? Why do people settle for less? Who are you ... or better yet ... <b>who do you <i>want</i> to be?</b><br><br>I loved the writing style. My book has about 4 or 5 dozen sticky notes highlighting my favorite passages! Lots of fabulous imagery. Very poetic. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397799499i/9329903._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am so <b>grateful</b> to have been allowed advance access to this fabulous book! <b>Karina Halle</b> ... what can I say? I think I love you ... not in a creepy, stalkerish kind of way ... just in a totally normal, you are my idol kind of way ... wait ... is that creepy? lol <br>Oh well! <b>It's true!</b> <br><br><br><br><b>Pre-Read</b><br><br> <b>OMG, OMG, OMG!!! A cover &amp; blurb! Ahhhhhhhh! So fucking excited!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389227612i/8008012._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>“Show me the stars again,” he said. His eyes speared me like nothing else, his face becoming dangerously handsome.<br><br>I looked up to the clear sky, to see the stars, but he reached out and grabbed my hand. His touch was hot, like his fingers were searing into my skin, that feeling of entering a hot tub on a cold night. I couldn’t help the shiver that ran gently down my spine.<br><br>“Not those stars,” he said huskily, leaning forward. His lips were wet and slightly open. “Your stars. Why I call you Estrella.”<br><br>I swallowed hard, my pulse burning along. I turned around in my chair so my back was to him and lifted up my hair, gathering it on the top of my head.<br><br>His chair scraped loudly on the ground as he got up, a sound that struck a new kind of fear in me.<br><br>No. Not fear.<br><br>Anticipation.<br><br>READ MORE: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://experimentinterror.com/2014/01/07/cover-reveal-excerpt-blurb-for-love-in-english/">http://experimentinterror.com/2014/01...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8381541444872741781" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1947100504" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1947100504" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1947100504?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=out-of-focus">out-of-focus</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=cheating-involved">cheating-involved</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1947100504" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2243698657557269521">3 out of 2,5<br/><br/><b>This book is out of focus...</b><br/><br/><b>Here is what happens:</b><br/>-	Married guy (38) meets a girl (23) and falls in love with her<br/>-	The girl falls in love with him too, although she tries not to, knowing he is married with a child. She even sleeps with another guy one night just to make her own point!!!! She wants to show that they are impossible.<br/>-	Normally, he lives in Spain, she lives in Canada. <br/>-	She is actually a student, he is a businessman (he was a footballer before but he got injured and quitt</span>
  <span id="freeText2243698657557269521" style="display:none">3 out of 2,5<br><br><b>This book is out of focus...</b><br><br><b>Here is what happens:</b><br>-	Married guy (38) meets a girl (23) and falls in love with her<br>-	The girl falls in love with him too, although she tries not to, knowing he is married with a child. She even sleeps with another guy one night just to make her own point!!!! She wants to show that they are impossible.<br>-	Normally, he lives in Spain, she lives in Canada. <br>-	She is actually a student, he is a businessman (he was a footballer before but he got injured and quitted).<br>-	She is tattooed and pierced with a rebel look, he wears suits and looks classier. On paper they do not look like a good match. <br>-	They meet in a program for adults practicing their conversational English and they spend one month together in the same camp in Spain.<br>-	They fight with their feelings internally for a month, trying to keep things on a friendly level only; however, they fail in the end. <br>-	They make love in the very last few days. That is when he cheats on his wife... And I would be pissed if he went on like this keeping her as a secret mistress while keeping his marriage safe at the same time. However, they separate their ways first but he wants her to never give up on their love and then, he goes and files for divorce. <br>-	Then, we read the painful process of divorce. <br>-	One the one side, our heroine feels guilty most of the time and she often whines. She also feels very insecure for some reasons.<br>-	On the other side, the hero tries to act strategically because he wants a peaceful divorce to be able to get the shared custody of his daughter. Thus, while trying to keep his new love, he also tries to keep things good with his soon-to-be-ex-wife, as well.<br>-	Naturally, ugly things happen and the new love is tested a few times. When it is tested, neither the hero nor the heroine acted as I wish they would have.<br>-	Eventually, there is a happy end for the new couple.<br><br><b>What bothered me was only one thing:</b><br><br>IT WAS OUT OF FOCUS!<br><br>This book would have been so much better if the writer had focused on either<br><br><b>“the idea of cheating”</b> and show its ugly consequences and how the innocent people in the story later end up with some new love (with some “non-cheating bastards”) <br><br>or <br><br><b>“a story of unavoidable forbidden love”</b>, in which a married person falls in love with someone else and this new love wins over no matter what the circumstances<br><br>I could accept either of them…<br><br>***********************************************<br><br>However, here, the book is a mess and it reflects the confused mind of the writer.<br><br>In one chapter, the writer tries to makes us see how unavoidable their love is, how deep and real their feelings are and how strong their chemistry is etc.<br><br>In another chapter, she writes about all these feelings of guilt, slut shaming and name calling, accusing the girl of being a homewrecker etc. (even her mother and sister call her names, including she herself doing it on her own all the time)<br><br>It really annoyed me and I didn’t know how to feel.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br>What I am trying to say here is if you are going to make this new love win over, you shouldn’t taint it so much. The writer taints it!<br><br>She should have created more stable characters, making them behave in a way to make us believe that their love is really so big that it is unavoidable whatever the consequences are.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br>There are very nice touchy sentences in the book while they are explaining their feelings but I somehow didn’t feel their “so-called great love”. I couldn’t relate to either the hero or the heroine. <br><br>Maybe it was because they weren’t strong enough characters or maybe because the writer made a mess of the “big love” and the “moral values”, not knowing which one to focus on most and ending up ruining both!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490387410i/22309213.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The book is told by the heroine's point of view only. Maybe, it is one of the reasons why it always felt lacking. I was never in his head.<br><br>Also the book is nearly 400 hundred pages and it is really slow and dragging.<br><br><b>P.S. </b>If cheating is not one of your triggers and you can read books in which cheating is involved, then maybe you should try the ones worth the pain and the suffering such as "My time in the Affair" by Stylo Fantome or "A Love So Tragic" by Stevie J. Cole... They are truly amazing!<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>One last word about cheating in general:</b><br><br>I do not have a personal experience and I hope I never will but I don’t believe in putting the shame on the other woman. <br><br>If a husband cheats on his wife, he is the one who is betraying, not some woman who doesn’t know the wife at all. <br><br>And in a situation like this, rather than slut shaming the other woman, calling her “homewrecker”, maybe the wife should question what was wrong in their marriage or if there is nothing wrong, then, she should get angry with the one who really deserves her anger: <b>“the husband”</b>, not the other woman. <br><br>Just saying...</span>
  <a data-text-id="2243698657557269521" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4800294096484886873"><b>******6++++ Estrellas Brillantes******</b><br/><br/><i>(BR With My book club babes, Patty, Alex, Carmen, and Rosita)</i><br/><br/>There are not enough stars to rate this book, for me this was pure perfection. A blazing story about a passionate love; the kind we all dream and fantasize about. Karina Halle words gripped my heart and emotions from the moment I started reading. Wow! truly captivating... <br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/f66f1b6e-5fbe-402b-a58a-23be9170631f_zps3ef35071.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418335897i/12751175.jpg' alt=' photo f66f1b6e-5fbe-402b-a58a-23be9170631f_zps3ef35071.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Vera Miles is a twenty three year old woman from Canada, backpacking through Europe, looking for an aventure. Her last stop </span>
  <span id="freeText4800294096484886873" style="display:none"><b>******6++++ Estrellas Brillantes******</b><br><br><i>(BR With My book club babes, Patty, Alex, Carmen, and Rosita)</i><br><br>There are not enough stars to rate this book, for me this was pure perfection. A blazing story about a passionate love; the kind we all dream and fantasize about. Karina Halle words gripped my heart and emotions from the moment I started reading. Wow! truly captivating... <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/f66f1b6e-5fbe-402b-a58a-23be9170631f_zps3ef35071.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418335897i/12751175.jpg" alt=" photo f66f1b6e-5fbe-402b-a58a-23be9170631f_zps3ef35071.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Vera Miles is a twenty three year old woman from Canada, backpacking through Europe, looking for an aventure. Her last stop is Spain, she's joining a program where she will work in a program, helping Spaniards practice their conversational skills in english, for exchange of a room and food in a gorgeous resort, four hours outside Madrid. In Las Palabras Resort she meets the gorgeous Mateo Casalles; he's a former soccer player, thirty eight years old and married. Mateo and Vera, bond instantly, they become fast friends, the comfort and intimacy between them urges them both to open up about all the things about their lives they don't dare to tell anyone. The sexual tension is palpable and constant between them, but neither of them want to act on it, respecting Mateo's marriage vows. Vera does everything possible to sabotage her feelings for him, but the heart wants what it wants and on the last few days together before they both have to go back to the real world, they both have no more strength left and finally surrender to a passionate affair. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/1ffc46e3-de35-4812-a25a-67a23f1c5754_zps57967ae8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418335897i/12751176.jpg" alt=" photo 1ffc46e3-de35-4812-a25a-67a23f1c5754_zps57967ae8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Vera goes back to Canada, but not as the same woman that first left, not only did she find love, but friends and a wonderful place where she felt like she truly belonged, something she's been yearning to feel her whole life. Life is miserable for both Mateo and Vera, their love burns deep and they are ready to just be together without thinking of the consequences. Mateo is in loveless marriage where the only thing keeping him is his daughter and Vera lives her life without any real purpose in it. Life together won't be easy, is deep love and burning passion enough for a relationship to work? Will they make the ultimate sacrifices and fight for their universe of love and stars?<br><br>I've always had a deep love for all things Spain, when I visit it's gets even harder to leave, each time. The music, the food, the art, the people; everything about that country fascinates me and Karina Halle did a magnificent job describing the beautiful setting. Her words transported me to Spain, making me feel every emotion in the story and engraving the words of her novel deep in my heart. Don't waste any time and read this book, truly romantic and passionate, a masterpiece!!!!!<br><br>My <i>Love, in English</i> music playlist:<br>*Entre Dos Aguas by Paco De Lucia<br>*Girl of Fire by Alicia Keys<br>*You Can't always Get What You Want by The Rolling Stones<br>*Barcelona by Giulia y Los Tellarini<br>*Explosions by Ellie Goulding<br>*A Sky Full of Stars by Coldplay</span>

<div id="review_917299482" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/917299482" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/917299482?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cotton-candy-romance">cotton-candy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=oh-the-angst">oh-the-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=is-getting-hot-in-here">is-getting-hot-in-here</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer917299482" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4026030938531182561"><b>4,5 Brightly Burning Stars.</b><br/><br/><i>”I’m starting to think that most villains aren’t evil—they are just misunderstood. Or victims of that most manipulative force: love.” </i><br/><br/>What happens when two worlds collide? <br/>Vera is a 23 years old Canadian girl, she enters on an English program in Spain. She believe she’s going to have the experience of her life. (And well, she will.) <br/>Mateo is a 38 year old, businessman, married and with a 5 year old daughter. He doesn’t have any feelings for his wife anymore, he only st</span>
  <span id="freeText4026030938531182561" style="display:none"><b>4,5 Brightly Burning Stars.</b><br><br><i>”I’m starting to think that most villains aren’t evil—they are just misunderstood. Or victims of that most manipulative force: love.” </i><br><br>What happens when two worlds collide? <br>Vera is a 23 years old Canadian girl, she enters on an English program in Spain. She believe she’s going to have the experience of her life. (And well, she will.) <br>Mateo is a 38 year old, businessman, married and with a 5 year old daughter. He doesn’t have any feelings for his wife anymore, he only stays with her for the sake of her daughters happiness, so when Vera appears in his life, his world is shaken. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398179665i/9381146._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They both start a fight with their own heart. But eventually they both lose. <br>And when real life, real feelings, family’s values and different life-styles get on their way, how long can they keep fighting? <br>Not all love stories are easy. Not all of them seems to be right from the beginning. Not all of them get an immediate happy ever after. Sometimes a beautiful love story endures a long and hurtful path to get to that point. And isn’t that what makes them remarkable? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4,5 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> For a contemporary romance it’s amazingly refreshing. This a beautiful love story, with angst enough to frustrate us and keep us interested. The age gap was a little hard for me, I don’t like them when they’re too big, but eventually I got past that. This was probably one of the bests NA books I’ve read recently. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> First person. Addictive, emotional and beautiful. Karina Halle always deliver a book amazingly. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> Vera was pretty good, I liked her from the begging. She never was a villain to me, just got caught up in live. Mateo was also very good and refreshing. I also loved him. The supportive characters were also pretty good. 	<br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot moments. <br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_758916718" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/758916718" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/758916718?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer758916718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3882373525125135168"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> Love, In English<br/><b>Series:</b> No. Standalone.<br/><b>Author:</b> Karina Halle<br/><b>Release Date: </b> April 20, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 3 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Karina Halle is one of my favorite authors; her books are always exciting, full of suspense and have the best yet the weirdest romances ever. I simply adore her! My love for her books made me break my number one rule. – I don’t deliberately read books with adultery. And look at me now, here I am rating and reviewing Love, In Engl</span>
  <span id="freeText3882373525125135168" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Love, In English<br><b>Series:</b> No. Standalone.<br><b>Author:</b> Karina Halle<br><b>Release Date: </b> April 20, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 3 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Karina Halle is one of my favorite authors; her books are always exciting, full of suspense and have the best yet the weirdest romances ever. I simply adore her! My love for her books made me break my number one rule. – I don’t deliberately read books with adultery. And look at me now, here I am rating and reviewing Love, In English completely manipulated by my fixation with Dex, Javier and Camden.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398350769i/9404758.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have known from the very beginning that Love, In English would be very hard read for me. That’s why I anxiously read all the teasers and reviews of it. I wanted to be prepared. I wanted to know if this book will break me, make me cry or if it will make me angry. Karina Halle’s books are too good to be missed, so I tried to make myself mentally ready for the heartbreak. That was my mistake. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398350882i/9404767.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I simply knew too much about the story! How could I enjoy it properly while I had known very well how this story would go? From the first page I knew what was going on, so nothing really surprised me and for the most part I was bored…That’s why I won’t be saying much about the plot, if you haven’t already read Love, In English, please do yourself a favor and don’t read too many reviews, especially when they summarize the plot. <br><br>Anyway, It’s hard for me to review Love, In English. Giving this exceptional tale of forbidden love only a three stars is making my heart ache, but I can’t give it more :( I didn’t have much problems with cheating, as I was ready for that. So please, know that this is not why I rated Love, In English three stars. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398350769i/9404760.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While Karina’s writing touched my heart and seriously amazed me once again, I found it hard to feel deeply connected to the characters. Even though I liked Vera, I hadn’t been in sync with her. As for Mateo, I just felt like he was one of those guys who wanted to feel young again and took it to completely another level. He acted like gigantic ass more than once. I was not able to agree with their decision, and it has nothing to do with cheating per se. It was actions that followed that made me angry at them. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398350769i/9404761.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, this story just wasn’t for me. Not very bad, nor as splendid as other Karina Halle’s books, Love, In English lacked something that could make me feel everything. The tale of Mateo and Vera’s relationship was harsh, and yes it was very realistic and beautiful in kind of ugly way, that will definitely appeal to many readers. Unfortunately, despite those qualities, I just couldn’t find myself in this book. I think I was this little, clueless girl standing in the corner trying to understand and not judge while still being not mature to get the drama wholeheartedly. <br><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK <span id="freeTextContainer12650925217046713543">I am a huge Karina Halle fan. I discovered her with her Experiment in Terror series and didn't sleep for about two weeks as I devoured them one by one. When Love, In English came out I bought it immediately and I've been sneaking little pieces of it whenever I can, like the chocolate I hide from my kids in my underwear drawer. I haven't wanted it to end because then I will miss it. I will miss Vera and Mateo. And I will miss Karina. She writes effortlessly and the story flows that way, making yo</span>
  <span id="freeText12650925217046713543" style="display:none">I am a huge Karina Halle fan. I discovered her with her Experiment in Terror series and didn't sleep for about two weeks as I devoured them one by one. When Love, In English came out I bought it immediately and I've been sneaking little pieces of it whenever I can, like the chocolate I hide from my kids in my underwear drawer. I haven't wanted it to end because then I will miss it. I will miss Vera and Mateo. And I will miss Karina. She writes effortlessly and the story flows that way, making you forget you are reading, making you forget there really isn't a Mateo out there (yes there is, damn it!) in a sun-soaked country just waiting for me, I mean, Vera.<br /><br />I could do a book recap, but others have done it so much better than I have time to do here. Simply put, Karina's books are in a league of their own, always, and her work speaks for itself. This book is taut, emotional, and sexy. And I simply loved it.</span>

    <a title="Claire Contreras" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10054133-claire-contreras"><img alt="Claire Contreras" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544066540p2/10054133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/891940171?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Claire Contreras" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Claire Contreras" href="/user/show/10054133-claire-contreras">Claire Contreras</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer891940171" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16097631057483725367">I’m a fan of “forbidden” romances, but I’m equally as hesitant to read them since they can go either way. Sometimes I love them, other times I loathe them. Karina Halle has managed to take a difficult subject and shed a beautiful light on it. <br/><br/>Love in English is not a love story, but a story about love. <br/><br/>Real love. <br/><br/>The soul mate, you know they’re meant to be together kind of love that doesn’t give you any other option but to root for them even if you know the circumstances are less than ideal. <br/><br/>Lik</span>
  <span id="freeText16097631057483725367" style="display:none">I’m a fan of “forbidden” romances, but I’m equally as hesitant to read them since they can go either way. Sometimes I love them, other times I loathe them. Karina Halle has managed to take a difficult subject and shed a beautiful light on it. <br /><br />Love in English is not a love story, but a story about love. <br /><br />Real love. <br /><br />The soul mate, you know they’re meant to be together kind of love that doesn’t give you any other option but to root for them even if you know the circumstances are less than ideal. <br /><br />Like all of Karina’s prior books, Love in English is a story, a journey in which the characters take their own turbulent roads to finding themselves and in turn, each other. I may have been a little worried about the subject when I started reading this, but by the end of it I had stars in my eyes.<br /><br />It's angsty, it's sexy, it's swoon-worthy, it's written beautifully, it's Love...In English ;). <br /><br />If i haven't convinced you yet...<br /><br /><b> I raised my brows. “Love, in English, is love…”<br />“What is it in Spanish?”<br />I was so enthralled by his hypnotic eyes, I could barely remember. “Amore?”<br />He shook his head ever so slightly. “No. Love in Spanish is you.” <b><br /><br /><br />If there was a word for "swoon" in Spanish, I would insert it right here. </b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16097631057483725367" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
