  <span id="freeText11514302671156084470" style="display:none"><b>5 Estrellas Untranslated<br><br><i>Love knows not distance; it hath no continent; its eyes are for the stars</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398585230i/9437715.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Compelling<br>Emotional <br>Fierce<br>Real<br><br>A love story with a KH twist, flair and talent.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398585230i/9437716._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Vera Miles</b> the self-appointed villain in her own love story and <b>Mateo Casalles</b> the former soccer star Spaniard, married and lost in the daily stress and chaos, despaired and let down by their own families will find the stars in each others eyes and their souls will be reunited. Can love suffer distance and betrayal?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398585230i/9437717.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>From Canada to London and then Spain, Vera is narrating her life, her side of the story. I was engrossed and in love with her and the surroundings, with the people she met and the sky she was gazing at at night. Sometimes I felt like a voyeur, others like was reading her innermost thoughts in her journal. But most of the times, <b>I was</b> Vera Miles. A woman in love with a married man, thousand of miles away from home. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398585230i/9437718.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4785031.Karina_Halle" title="Karina Halle" rel="nofollow noopener">Karina Halle</a>'s first attempt in contemporary romance made my heart ache and my soul sing.<br>Fascinating characters that are her norm with a hero twist and a villain complex. Unusual, unique setting and a really simple plot consist this must read romance.<br>Karina shares that she found inspiration from personal experience, but she is not Vera nor Mateo. I am envy of her. I want to pack my bags and take my fiance for a trip to the stars, to explore and find ourselves and fall in love all over again in every language imaginable.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398585230i/9437719.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And a book that makes you dream, is an excellent one....<br><br><br><i> While I was waiting for the book, I was very excited!!</i><br><b>SQUEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE!!!!</b><br><br><i>ARC, in print, courtesy of the AMAZING <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4785031.Karina_Halle" title="Karina Halle" rel="nofollow noopener">Karina Halle</a>, in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381372245ra/4772368.gif" width="400" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>He’s thirty-eight. I’m twenty-three.<br><br>He speaks Spanish. I speak English.<br><br>He lives in Spain. I live in Canada.<br><br>He dresses in thousand-dollar suits. I’m covered in tattoos.<br><br>He’s married and has a five-year old daughter.<br><br>I’m single and can’t commit to anyone or anything.</b>

WHAT ELSE DO YOU NEED?!?!?!?!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434746i/877845.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4676969-natalie?shelf=summer-2020">summer-2020</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer908108404" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10095698866118410303"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448490597i/17149311.jpg' width='400' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1524519920i/25423713._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“You and I, we were always a memory in the making.” </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><b>★★★★ ! </b>Love, in English, book 1. Amazing, beautiful, spellbinding. A married, father falls for his exact opposite in Vera, half his age. Best read of year 2014!<br/><br/>Karina Halle at her best! I love, love romances with a traveling- theme, and reading Love, in English was a magical experience for me. <br/>It made want to take the next plain to Spain. it's not often a book compels me like Love, in English did. Epic!<br/>I absolutely loved Vera and Mateo's lo</span>
  <span id="freeText10095698866118410303" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448490597i/17149311.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1524519920i/25423713._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You and I, we were always a memory in the making.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>★★★★ ! </b>Love, in English, book 1. Amazing, beautiful, spellbinding. A married, father falls for his exact opposite in Vera, half his age. Best read of year 2014!<br><br>Karina Halle at her best! I love, love romances with a traveling- theme, and reading Love, in English was a magical experience for me. <br>It made want to take the next plain to Spain. it's not often a book compels me like Love, in English did. Epic!<br>I absolutely loved Vera and Mateo's love story! This book was impossible from page one to put down. The writing and plot pulled me in instantly. <br>Love, in English is my absolute favorite kind of book. <br>A forbidden love story, with a big age difference in an exotic setting, not to mention a kick ass heroine and a swoon worthy, over-the-charge sexy hero. <br>It involves cheating, and it usually makes me sick to read about, but not in this one.<br><br>Mateo. Swoon, SWOON! <br>He is the older, sexy, wealthy ex-footballer with a sexy accent and Vera is the significantly younger, covered in tattoos, Canadanian he meets during a month in sunny Spain. <br>He wants to learn English better and she teaches adults. <br>Sparks fly immediately but he is married, a father and almost twice her age. <br>And he lives in Spain. How can it possibly work? <br><br>Love, in English is written entirely from Vera's point of view. <br>I loved every second of being in her head, she really is a kickass heroine and I'm so grateful to Karina Halle for writing this. <br>Love, in English was so awesom that it has bumped Karina to one of my favorite authors and it was by far my best read in all 2014. <br>I can't stress enough how much I loved the hero in this. Mateo...sigh......<br><br>The sexual tension between him and Vera was off- the- charts! <br>He made my knees go weak. Karina Halle, thank you for writing this. The writing was amazing, the characters were amazing and the plot was amazing. <br>I'm already looking forward to all the epic rereads of Love, in English. <br>I can't tell you enough how much I loved this! <br><b>READ IT ASAP!</b></span>

<div id="review_755364440" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/755364440" />
    <a title="Brenna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna"><img alt="Brenna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580475762p2/12928663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755364440?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brenna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brenna" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna">Brenna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=top-top-fave">top-top-fave</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=ugly-cry">ugly-cry</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755364440" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2283616835977679410"><b>It's officially LIVE!</b><br/>Amazon ➔ <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1i5S45v'>http://amzn.to/1i5S45v</a><br/>B&N ➔<a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://bit.ly/LiE-Nook'>http://bit.ly/LiE-Nook</a><br/><br/><b><i>Love, in English</i> is a powerful story of finding love and finding yourself in the most unexpected places. It’s been a long time since a contemporary romance stole my heart and put me in a such a major book funk afterwards quite like this one did.</b><br/><br/>Vera, a twenty-three year old Canadian astronomy student is on her way to Spain. She has signed up for a program teaching conversational English to businessmen and woman. On th</span>
  <span id="freeText2283616835977679410" style="display:none"><b>It's officially LIVE!</b><br />Amazon ➔ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1i5S45v">http://amzn.to/1i5S45v</a><br />B&amp;N ➔<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/LiE-Nook">http://bit.ly/LiE-Nook</a><br /><br /><b><i>Love, in English</i> is a powerful story of finding love and finding yourself in the most unexpected places. It’s been a long time since a contemporary romance stole my heart and put me in a such a major book funk afterwards quite like this one did.</b><br /><br />Vera, a twenty-three year old Canadian astronomy student is on her way to Spain. She has signed up for a program teaching conversational English to businessmen and woman. On the bus ride to their home for the next month, she meets the charming, enigmatic Mateo. As silly as it sounds, I can’t deny that I had the warm and fuzzies right from their first conversation. The chemistry, even as friends, between the two is completely unmistakable. <br /><br />This story takes you through Vera and Mateo’s life over the next month as they get to know each other, as well as many others at the program. They are forced to <i>talk</i> and talk A LOT. It’s an interesting dynamic to see these people from so many backgrounds having to converse and find common ground. It takes relationship building to a whole new level. <br /><br />The pacing of Vera and Mateo’s relationship is done with so much finesse. From the first chats, to the meaningful conversations, the building of feelings, and everything in between, I was hooked. I was hooked to these beautiful, flawed, charming kindred spirits who had no choice but to fall in love against all odds. It was written in the stars. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“When I know something, I know it. Now, I know what love is. And I love you. And I cannot imagine going back to the lie I had before, because that was no life at all. That was just existing. That was just chasing down the next day so I could feel it pass under me.” He placed his large hand over my heart. <b>“You made me stop chasing the days. You made me hold onto them.”</b></i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Besides the draw I had to these characters, I absolutely loved the setting. Spain is the perfect backdrop for such a beautiful story. I found it interesting; I wanted to learn more about everything, what they were doing, where they were going. It felt like I was there, like I could see the things they were seeing and it made everything feel even more <i>real</i>.<br /><br />It’s clear from the synopsis and the interactions between Mateo and Vera, that there is going to be some infidelity involved. I think this is a subject that is hard to take whether it’s real life or in fiction, but I can honestly say, I don’t think it could have been handled any better. It’s nothing done on a whim, without thinking, without meaning, it just seemed almost inevitable. I think knowing how Vera was struggling with her feelings of more than friendship from early on to witnessing it eating her up so completely as time went on, it made me feel for her. It was easy for me to relate to her and understand her feelings and actions. My issue with cheating in books is usually the back and forth and <i>unnecessary</i> angst, but here I never questioned the motives or intentions of either character. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>I couldn’t really go on like this, everyday a battle between my heart and my mind, between right and wrong, between the dreams and the reality.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Whether it was wrong or right, it certainly <i>felt</i> right to me. This whole book, every page, it felt right, it felt real. It’s unique, compelling, heartfelt, and well written. I’ve been hard pressed to find a romance that has all of those components and has made me care so deeply. This is truly a story that will stay with me. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Love, our love, had been a shooting star, burning in the darkness, unseen, until it got too close, too bright and too quick to capture. </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />5+ stars. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2283616835977679410" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_755369694" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/755369694" />
    <a title="Ali " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5847230-ali"><img alt="Ali " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1553184305p2/5847230.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755369694?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ali " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ali " href="/user/show/5847230-ali">Ali </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5847230-ali?shelf=cry-baby">cry-baby</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755369694" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1397721880470794401"><br/><br/>I need to be upfront with something. I hate adultery in books.  I'm not opposed to cheating in books, but adultery is a trigger for me.  I don't usually gravitate towards them.  Why? Because I think marriage is a truly special thing and its importance has been tarnished over the years.  Too often people enter it lightly or don't respect the commitment of it.  It is something that aggravates me, but that is just my issue and in no way a judgment on anyone else.<br/><br/><br/><br/>That being said, I had some trepidat</span>
  <span id="freeText1397721880470794401" style="display:none"><br /><br />I need to be upfront with something. I hate adultery in books.  I'm not opposed to cheating in books, but adultery is a trigger for me.  I don't usually gravitate towards them.  Why? Because I think marriage is a truly special thing and its importance has been tarnished over the years.  Too often people enter it lightly or don't respect the commitment of it.  It is something that aggravates me, but that is just my issue and in no way a judgment on anyone else.<br /><br /><br /><br />That being said, I had some trepidation entering Love, In English.  I was afraid I would hate Mateo.  Not for being a married man who falls in love with another woman.  I don't blame anyone for matters of the heart.  But for acting on those feelings, that is what I feared would make me dislike him and never root for him as a love interest. Dislike him for not ending a marriage before starting a relationship with someone else.  Again, this is a personal trigger.<br /><br /><br /><br />I could not be more happy to say, I did not hate Mateo.  I didn't even ever dislike him.  Not even a little.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Love, In English isn't a story that focuses on the affair.  It's a story that focuses on two lonely people who just happen to find their soulmate in an unlikely place and at an imperfect time.  Vera and Mateo don't mean to fall in love.  Vera very much fights her feelings, riddled with guilt from the start, when it is just a slight attraction.<br /><br /><br /><br />This is very much a coming of age story for Vera.  She finds herself, where she truly belongs and some very hard life lessons. She also learns what it is to love and that love is never, ever an easy thing. <br /><br /><br /><br />Mateo also finds himself. Realizing that the life he leads is anything but fulfilling. He's become complacent with it.  His marriage may not be horrible, his life may be comfortable, his career successful,  but those things don't equate to happiness.<br /><br /><br /><br />Mateo and Vera's affair is not started up lightly, it isn't frivolous.  It is two somewhat empty hearts colliding with the only thing that can fill them up.   Because of the feelings they have for one another, Mateo really does try to do the right thing, if maybe a bit late.  Falling out of love, however, is just as hard and messy as falling in love.  A lesson Mateo and Vera both very much learn in Love, In English.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br />I have to say that this is the most emotional and beautiful book Halle has written.  She's written great love stories before but there was nothing else to distract you here, no horror, no action. This is all emotions, real and gritty and hard.<br /><br /><br /><br />Applause to Karina Halle for doing two things few have been able to. One, she made me overcome the adultery. Easily, in fact. I was rooting for Mateo and Vera pretty early on. How can you not hope two lost souls find themselves in each other?  Two, she made me cry. Three times, in fact.<br /><br /><br /><br />I hope this is a genre she will pick up again in the future, it's a good one for her. I also hope that anyone who is like me, shies away from adultery or cheating, will give this book a shot. It may surprise you.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1397721880470794401" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_890473992" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/890473992" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/890473992?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-i-o">authors-i-o</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=favorites-books">favorites-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer890473992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9304003395860184496"><blockquote>
  <b>Intoxicating!!! Unique!!! Special!!!</b>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472401.jpg' alt='Love in English by Karina Halle photo images9_zps1fc9ee00.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote> I have been unable to get this book out of my head since I finished the last word…and the beauty of the writing by this author ……just extraordinary, just astonishing!<br/><blockquote>
  <b>“What is love? In English.”<br/>I raised my brows. “Love, in English, is love?”<br/>“What is it in Spanish?”<br/>I was so enthralled by his hypnotic eyes, I could barely remember. “Amore?”<br/>He shook his head ever so slightly. “No. Love in Spanish is you.”</b>
</blockquote><br/>Vera Miles arrives in Spain to take up </span>
  <span id="freeText9304003395860184496" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>Intoxicating!!! Unique!!! Special!!!</b>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472401.jpg" alt="Love in English by Karina Halle photo images9_zps1fc9ee00.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> I have been unable to get this book out of my head since I finished the last word…and the beauty of the writing by this author ……just extraordinary, just astonishing!<br><blockquote>
  <b>“What is love? In English.”<br>I raised my brows. “Love, in English, is love?”<br>“What is it in Spanish?”<br>I was so enthralled by his hypnotic eyes, I could barely remember. “Amore?”<br>He shook his head ever so slightly. “No. Love in Spanish is you.”</b>
</blockquote><br>Vera Miles arrives in Spain to take up a summer job. Spending a few weeks teaching conversational English to Spanish business people and enjoying the free room and meals, meeting new people sounds like an experience from heaven. She does all that but what she never expected was to fall in love. <br><br>Mateo, a businessman from Madrid, is gorgeous, sexy and married. But he finds himself being drawn towards a woman he never imagined would be someone he could connect with. His unhappy in his marriage, he and his wife have grown apart and the only thing that is still keeping them together, is their daughter. He never imagined that he could find that something he had lost for years, again.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“You can fall in love in a second,” she said with a snap of her fingers. “The heart has no regard for time.”</b>
</blockquote>The subject of cheating with a married man is certainly not something I like reading about. But what is incredible is how the author handled the “taboo “so well. What stood out for me was the emotional connection they had from the beginning and how they battled to not give in to the deep feelings and love that slowly grew to a point that they could no longer resist giving in to something that was meant to be. <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472402.jpg" alt="Love in English by Karina Halle photo LIE_zpsb2cb828a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> You feel their love, their pain, their uncertainty, their heartbreak. Her characters are unforgettable. You become emotionally involved with them from the very beginning. <br>Vera Miles has a place in my heart. Beautiful, dreamer, tattooed and pierced, lonely and somewhat lost…afraid to love…..<blockquote>
  <b>You are lonely, but you say you like to be alone.”<br>I nodded. “I do. I prefer it. But… it doesn’t mean I don’t want someone to love me.” My eyes stung, as if tears were on their way. I bit my lip, debating if I should say more. “It doesn’t mean that I don’t have a lot of love in me to give someone.” </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved the goodness in her, struggling with the feelings she has for Mateo and wanting to do the right thing <br>.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472403.jpg" alt=" photo images10_zps8617c7b8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br>A beautiful dreamer with such heart.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472404.jpg" alt="Love in English by Karina Halle photo e76fe445ae95b328e93c8d0be51d9b5d_zps84f65e88.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br>Mateo Casalles, mature, passionate, sensitive, caring, loving….his sensuality….I fell in love with this man and he’s wound himself around my heart forever. I felt a deep connection with him. He’s likeable, lovable and totally irresistible!!<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472405.jpg" alt="Love in English by Karina Halle photo edcda5bfcdd05e5944152b055f192d95_zps445892f4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br>And in some way, just like Vera, has lost his way….<blockquote>&lt;<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472406.jpg" alt="Love in English by Karina Halle photo bd96d8b9d97f27c80f90cb1b877fbcf1_zps65139b7a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote>Powerful writing….the consequences of their love is filled with emotion, heartbreak, pain….and you feel it all because it’s such so real ….we can relate to all the chaos that ensues.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472407.jpg" alt="Love in English by Karina Halle photo 90a2b14a37ce98f1f32ed5bf3c996c15_zps58eabf6f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> But in the end, love does overcome everything……..<b>“But love makes you an optimist,” she said. “That is what love is. It is hope for the future. Love doesn’t want you to lose faith, to view the world darkly, to have no hope. Love makes you believe in the impossible. That is the meaning of the word.”</b>The vivid imagery, the settings…I felt the heat, heard the music, tasted the food, touched the stars, smelt the air that was all Spain……the town of Acantilado<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472408.jpg" alt="Love in English by Karina Halle photo __serviciosviajesolympiacom_fotos_Benidorm_PUEBLOACANTILADO_vistafachada_zps1596bc59.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>And beautiful Madrid <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472409.jpg" alt="Love in English by Karina Halle photo images11_zpsdb72875b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>A beautiful book that made me feel so many emotions. Read it and feel it!!<br><br>I want to share something I found that reminded me of Vera Miles and her free spirit!!<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398859848i/9472410.jpg" alt="Love in English by Karina Halle photo 6030607844b97e37ffa5b73c66e13cc5_zpsa2186f5f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="9304003395860184496" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZaKa0iVz2XjR1WgsrHExERJ6xuFHQ7uiUYtWlg8XO1oXdsASrtottBdb3HWlsuYFhJ5q+Mofd3wbq9xrTGVPqg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OUJZCG7Vx3+q+sHMFx9jjdRB+FU+UyV5hK5nIyteH/9LlgPI5Xwzs2x0dZUe3LSZQqVUTLMP6afOju3eaCxrDw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer10107971501463086496">Karina Halle is a screenwriter, a former music & travel journalist, and the New York Times, Wall Street Journal, and USA Today bestselling author of The Pact, A Nordic King, and Sins & Needles, as well as sixty other wild and romantic reads. <br/><br/>She, her musician husband, and their adopted pit bull, Bruce, live in a rainforest on an island off the coast of British Columbia, where they operate Raven Ri</span>
  <span id="freeText10107971501463086496" style="display:none">Karina Halle is a screenwriter, a former music &amp; travel journalist, and the New York Times, Wall Street Journal, and USA Today bestselling author of The Pact, A Nordic King, and Sins &amp; Needles, as well as sixty other wild and romantic reads. <br /><br />She, her musician husband, and their adopted pit bull, Bruce, live in a rainforest on an island off the coast of British Columbia, where they operate Raven Ridge, a B&amp;B that’s perfect for writers’ retreats and romantic getaways. <br /><br />In the winter, you can often find them in California or on their beloved island of Kauai, soaking up as much sun (and getting as much inspiration) as possible. For more information, visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.authorkarinahalle.com/books">www.authorkarinahalle.com/books</a>.<br /><br />Halle is represented by Root Literary and is both self-published, and published by Simon &amp; Schuster, Hachette, Penguin, and Montlake. Her books have been published in numerous languages around the world.<br /><br />Karina isn't on Goodreads and does NOT check her messages here - please contact her via Instagram (@authorhalle) instead :)<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
